cd /root/freebsd; TOOLS_PREFIX=/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp  INSTALL="sh /root/freebsd/tools/install.sh"  PATH=/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp/legacy/usr/sbin:/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp/legacy/usr/bin:/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp/legacy/bin:/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp/legacy/usr/libexec:/sbin:/bin:/usr/sbin:/usr/bin  WORLDTMP=/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp make  -f Makefile.inc1  DESTDIR=  OBJTOP='/usr/obj/root/freebsd/amd64.amd64/tmp/obj-kernel-tools'  OBJROOT='${OBJTOP}/'  MAKEOBJDIRPREFIX=  BOOTSTRAPPING=1200086  SSP_CFLAGS=  MK_HTML=no -DNO_LINT MK_MAN=no  -DNO_PIC MK_PROFILE=no -DNO_SHARED  -DNO_CPU_CFLAGS MK_RETPOLINE=no MK_WARNS=no MK_CTF=no kernel-tools
